					value = 0.015
				}
				GER_add_eu_fed = yes
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_global_flag = GER_EU_federalized_global
					}
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							is_puppet_of = FROM
						}
						PREV = {
							get_current_government_type = yes
							GER = {
								puppet = PREV
							}
							restore_previous_government_type = yes
						}
					}
					GER = {

							target = FROM
							transfer_troops = yes
						}
					}
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_core_of = FROM
						}
						add_core_of = GER
					}
				}
				else = {
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							is_puppet_of = FROM
						}
						PREV = {
							get_current_government_type = yes
							GER = {
								puppet = PREV
							}
							restore_previous_government_type = yes
						}
					}
					FROM = {
						get_current_government_type = yes
						GER = {
							puppet = FROM
						}
						restore_previous_government_type = yes
						set_country_flag = GER_country_joined_EU
						hidden_effect = { set_cosmetic_tag = GER_EUU }
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_temp_variable = {
					var = eu_fed_var_temp
					value = 0.005
				}
				GER_add_eu_fed = yes
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = GER_supporting_volt_europa
			FROM = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = social_liberal

					}

	ZZZ_mor_alg_war_timer = {

			}
		}

			always = no
		}

			MOR = {
				surrender_progress > 0.6
			}
		}

				surrender_progress > 0.6
			}
		}
		cancel_effect = { #Algerian Victory
			clr_global_flag = ALG_maghreb_war_global

			}

					}
				}

				}
